method="POST" route="/executions/retry"><h1 class="text-[1.75em] font-semibold">Retry Executions</h1><p class="mb-8 text-lg text-primary">Queue file executions to be retried.</p><div class="flex overflow-x-auto px-2 [&amp;&gt;div:first-child]:pr-2 [&amp;&gt;div:last-child:not(:first-child)]:pl-2 [&amp;&gt;div:not(:first-child):not(:last-child)]:px-2"><div><a class="operation-target inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 p-1.5 no-underline hover:text-tertiary" href="https://github.com/Stedi/openApi/blob/main/core.json#:~:text=&quot;operationId&quot;%3A%20&quot;RetryExecutions&quot;" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon text-tertiary"><path d="M4 18V14.3C4 13.4716 3.32843 12.8 2.5 12.8H2V11.2H2.5C3.32843 11.2 4 10.5284 4 9.7V6C4 4.34315 5.34315 3 7 3H8V5H7C6.44772 5 6 5.44772 6 6V10.1C6 10.9858 5.42408 11.7372 4.62623 12C5.42408 12.2628 6 13.0142 6 13.9V18C6 18.5523 6.44772 19 7 19H8V21H7C5.34315 21 4 19.6569 4 18ZM20 14.3V18C20 19.6569 18.6569 21 17 21H16V19H17C17.5523 19 18 18.5523 18 18V13.9C18 13.0142 18.5759 12.2628 19.3738 12C18.5759 11.7372 18 10.9858 18 10.1V6C18 5.44772 17.5523 5 17 5H16V3H17C18.6569 3 20 4.34315 20 6V9.7C20 10.5284 20.6716 11.2 21.5 11.2H22V12.8H21.5C20.6716 12.8 20 13.4716 20 14.3Z"></path></svg>OpenAPI spec</a></div></div></div><p>The endpoint queues file executions that match the criteria specified in <code>condition</code> for retry. This includes child executions generated from past retry attempts - all matching executions will be queued. You can use this endpoint to programmatically handle <code>file.failed</code> events.</p>
<p>The endpoint returns an empty response upon success. You can monitor the status of retries using the <a href="/docs/edi-platform/api-reference/core/get-pollingexecutions">Poll Executions</a> endpoint or through the Stedi portal.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="how-retries-work"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#how-retries-work"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>How retries work</a></h2>
<p>Stedi only retries each execution ID once. That&#x27;s because when you retry a file, Stedi creates a child execution with a new ID and links it to the original (parent) execution.</p>
<p>To retry a file multiple times, you&#x27;ll need to either pass the execution ID of the latest retry attempt to this endpoint or specify a matching <code>condition</code>. For example, if you specify that Stedi should retry all executions with a <code>status</code> of <code>FAILED</code>, Stedi will queue all executions matching that criterion, including the latest child execution in existing retry chains.</p>
<p>That retry execution is linked to the original execution through the following properties:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>parentExecutionId</code>: The ID of the execution&#x27;s parent execution, if it is part of a retry chain.</li>
<li><code>childExecutionId</code>: The ID of this execution&#x27;s child execution, if it is part of a retry chain.</li>
</ul>
<p>You can also review all of a file&#x27;s retry attempts in the Stedi portal.</p><div class="flex items-end justify-between gap-2"><h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group Stedi will retry all executions matching the given criteria. For example, you can retry all file executions with a <code>FAILED</code> status within a specific date range.</p>
<p>Note that Stedi only retries each <code>executionId</code> once. Each retry attempt is stored as a new file execution within Stedi. If you need to retry a file multiple times, you&#x27;ll need to pass the ID of the latest retry attempt to this endpoint.</p><details class="[&amp;[open]&gt;summary&gt;.arrow-down-icon]:rotate-180 size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The status of the execution.</p>
<ul>
<li>You can only retry executions with a <code>FAILED</code> or <code>IGNORED</code> status.</li>
<li>An execution is <code>COMPLETED</code> when Stedi has finished processing the file with no errors. If the file is an outbound file, a <code>COMPLETED</code> status also means that Stedi successfully delivered it to the configured connection.</li>
</ul><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 last:rounded-b-md first:rounded-t-md"><div aria-level="1"
